< review>
As of 11/20/18, this place is no longer Asian Garden 2. It is now called Uncle's Chinese Cuisine and is under new management.

I use to love this place back when it was Asian Garden but now it is newly renovated and has new owners. The place looks nice and when we went in to eat, it was not busy at all. Before My husband and I placed our order we asked the waitress if it was possible to order sweet and sour tofu or sesame tofu, things not on the menu and we were rudely told no. The reason why we asked for this is  because with previous owners we were able to get this even though it was not on their menu. My husband proceeds to order tofu with mixed vegetables, vegetable fried rice and egg rolls for himself and I ordered cream cheese wontons and vegetable chow mein. We also asked for tea. The first thing to come out was the fried rice and it was undercooked as hell. The second thing to come out was the tofu and it was just okay. Next to came out was the egg rolls and cream cheese wontons. I actually enjoyed the wontons. At this point, we were still not served tea but other people who came in after were given tea. A younger waiter came up and asked how everything was and we told him we have yet to receive our tea. After a while I finished my wontons and my husband finished his tofu, rice and egg rolls and THEY FORGOT ABOUT MY CHOW MEIN. During the whole time I was waiting for my chow mein I watched several people, including the waiters and waitress, stuffing their faces with food and messing with produce. My husband went to talk to one of the owners about the issue and she called the waitress over and she lied to her face about putting the order in because 10 minutes later it comes out under done and disgusting. When this place was Asian Garden, it use to get so much business from my family, my in-laws and my husband and I, this place along with the new owner will never get any of our business ever.</review>

<Review>I just ate here and was not impressed. I tried the Mushroom Chicken with fried rice and a bowl of Wor won Ton Soup. The mushrooms were fresh and big and the chicken was very soft and tender, but my Wor Won Ton Soup was brought with just won tons, a couple pieces of pork and cabbage. It had no flavor and if it wasn't for the fact that I had eaten the dish before I  would have never known that it was suppose to have SHRIMP AND IT NEEDS TO SIMMER SO THE BROTH CAN GET FLAVOR.
I asked them if it was suppose to have shrimp and he looked at me like I was crazy then he took the bowl to the back and put some big shrimp in it. I added soo sauce and let it sit while I finished my lunch plate.  It was still tasteless. I asked the waiter if he had anymore that had sat and simmer and he said no and that they have the same cook. The male and female waiters were very attentive, but having to pay for something that isn't good really spoiled my meal. I did not leave them a tip and asked for my change when I  paid the bill. <Rate>1</Rate><Review>If I could give zero or half a star, I would.
We rescued a German Shepherd a little over a year. We brought him to this clinic because it was recommended to us by someone who works at the shelter where we got him. He has idiopathic epilepsy and requires medication daily to prevent the seizures from happening. If he misses a dose he is likely to have Grand Mal seizures within days. We have had issues with the staff every time that we need his prescription renewed. They assure us that the order will be put in same day (within an hour or so) - and it never is. They take days to fax the prescription to our pharmacy and by then he is typically out of his medication or doesn't have enough for his full dose. It takes us calling the pharmacy to check to see if they have received the prescription, and then the office to see if they have sent it - multiple times a day until it gets done. We typically spend two to three days playing phone tag to get his prescription filled. You would think they would be on top of filling a medication that is so vital to his health.
The staff is rude and they do not look at his chart before seeing him. We have to re-explain everything about his history (even the medication that they are prescribing him and why), first to the assistant and then again to the vet when he comes in. The check ups are done lazily and they only take his temperature - they don't check anything else like most vets would during a check up unless we have specific issues we want to bring to their attention.
The ONLY reason I would consider giving them even a half of a star would be because they will work with your budget if it's a little tight.
Needless to say, we will be switching clinics very soon.</Review>< Pictures>

< Review>
Love this church! Attended for the past 17 years, they have made tons of changes, a lot of improvements! Currently undergoing construction in their main auditorium and are expecting a bigger and better main sanctuary. With their new youth pastor on board the church is undergoing improvements both outwardly and inwardly. Ushers are friendly, services are amazing, and worship is filled with the presence of God! Definitely a great place to meet new people who love God.

They provide a youth service in English every Thursday (@7:30pm) for both high school and college students, and then 3 services on Sundays. One at 9:00am (for older members) one at 12:00pm (for young married people, and kids, usually in English) and one at 6:30pm. Sunday morning services are usually in Russian, however they do provide english translations through ear phones that are provided in the back. The best service for English speakers would be our 12:00pm service and Thursday evening youth service:)

There is something going on at church every single day. There are opportunities to get involved in Choir, Band, Youth Ministries, Home Groups, Bible Schools, Sunday School, Teen Bible School, Cafe, and more with the leadership admin staff.

Bethany also has prayer nights every Monday and Friday evening @9;30pm. These are so filled with God's presence and people who love and care about each other.

Summer is also filled with Saturday Evening Services Outside and several other outdoor events as well as TONS of different summer camp opportunities for kids and teens of all ages.

This church has a lot to offer for those who are interested in getting involved and being a part of something big in the community!

Give us a visit, bring a friend, we'll be happy to have you!<//Review>

< Text>
Such an awesome experience. I spent my 30th birthday here. Initially I was going to have a private party but ended up canceling it so I did a bottomless brunch paint day instead. Setting up the private party and canceling it was very easy to do. The bottles brunch was $45 and worth every penny. You got two sizeable pieces of chicken and a big ole waffle and bottomless mimosas. They are not skimpy or stingy with the mimosas. Most people had between two and three because honestly, you came to paint not get drunk. The instruction is easy to follow, there's tons of laughter and it's a super safe space to be a black woman, though all are welcome. I will come back again and again. I'm in love with my painting and am still shocked by how great it turned out. I can't recommend it enough.< /Text>
